add_namespace = pacificstates
add_namespace = KX_california
add_namespace = calpeaceout

### 1937 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # Commonwealth Nomination
	id = pacificstates.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.1"}
	title = pacificstates.1.t
	desc = pacificstates.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = pacificstates.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Culbert Olson
		name = pacificstates.1.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_olson
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.2"}
	title = pacificstates.2.t
	desc = pacificstates.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # nominate Henry Wallace
		name = pacificstates.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_wallace
		country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.1
				days = 8
			}
		}	
	}
	option = { # nominate Hiram Johnson
		name = pacificstates.2.b
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_johnson
		country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.1
				days = 8
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # nominate Charles L. McNary
		name = pacificstates.2.c
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_mcnary
		country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.1
				days = 8
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # nominate CC Young
		name = pacificstates.2.e
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_young
		country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.1
				days = 8
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Norris
		name = pacificstates.2.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "George Norris" }
				has_global_flag = USA_president_norris
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_norris
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.1
				days = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Dem-Rep Primary

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Earl Warren

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_warren
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # William Gibbs McAdoo
		name = pacificstates.3.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_mccadoo
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Clarence D. Martin
		name = pacificstates.3.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_martin
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Charles A. Sprague
		name = pacificstates.3.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_sprague
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Manchester Boddy
		name = pacificstates.3.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_boddy
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # John Aiso
		name = pacificstates.3.h
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAL_aiso_ran
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_aiso
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep Landon
		name = pacificstates.3.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Alf Landon" }
				has_global_flag = USA_president_landon
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_landon
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Republican Primary
	id = pacificstates.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.4"}
	title = pacificstates.4.t
	desc = pacificstates.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Robert Taft
		name = pacificstates.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_taft
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Harry Chandler
		name = pacificstates.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_chandler
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Howard Hughes
		name = pacificstates.4.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CAL_hughes_in_power_flag
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_hughes
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Frank Merriam
		name = pacificstates.4.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_merriam
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Frank Knox
		name = pacificstates.4.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_knox
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Louis B. Mayer
		name = pacificstates.4.g
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_immigrant_presidents
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_meyer
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep Curtis
		name = pacificstates.4.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Charles Curtis" }
				has_global_flag = USA_president_curtis
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_curtis
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Democrat Primary
	id = pacificstates.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.5"}
	title = pacificstates.5.t
	desc = pacificstates.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Henry J. Kaiser
		name = pacificstates.5.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_kaiser
		}
			country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Charles Martin
		name = pacificstates.5.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_martin
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Walt Disney
		name = pacificstates.5.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = Walt_Disney_dead
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_disney
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.251
			days = 2
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Garner
		name = pacificstates.5.e
		trigger = {	
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "John Nance Garner" }
				has_global_flag = USA_garner_is_president
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_garner
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # John McGroarty
		name = pacificstates.5.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_mcgroarty
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Election
	id = pacificstates.6
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.6"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		}
	}
	title = pacificstates.6.t
	desc = pacificstates.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1937_election
			is_supposed_to_fire_for_tag = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_election_occured
			if = { # Upton Sinclair
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Upton Sinclair"
					desc = "POLITICS_UPTON_SINCLAIR_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Upton_Sinclair.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radical_progressivism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_an_end_to_poverty }
				}
			}
			if = { # Culbert Olson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_olson
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Culbert Olson"
					desc = "POLITICS_CULBERT_OLSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Culbert_Olson.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radsoc_humanistic_capitalism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_proud_atheist }
				}
			}
			if = { # Henry Wallace
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_wallace
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLACE_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = georgism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_world_planner }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles McNary
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_mcnary
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles McNary"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_MCNARY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Charles_L_McNary.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_agrarianism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_electrify_america }
				}
			}
			if = { # Hiram Johnson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_johnson
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hiram Johnson"
					desc = "POLITICS_HIRAM_JOHNSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Hiram_Johnson.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_radical_progressivism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_inward_reformer }
				}
			}
			if = { # C.C. Young
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_young
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "C.C. Young"
					desc = "POLITICS_CC_YOUNG_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_CC_Young.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_humanistic_capitalism_subtype
					traits = { diehard_progressive }
				}
			}
			if = { # George Norris
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_norris
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Norris"
					desc = "POLITICS_GEORGE_NORRIS_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_George_W_Norris.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_radical_progressivism_subtype
					traits = { the_fighting_liberal }
				}
			}
			if = { # Earl Warren
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_warren
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Earl Warren"
					desc = "POLITICS_EARL_WARREN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Earl_Warren.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radical_liberalism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_crusader_of_justice }
				}
			}
			if = { # William Gibbs McAdoo
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_mccadoo
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "William Gibbs McAdoo"
					desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_GIBBS_MCADOO_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_William_Gibbs_McAdoo.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = national_liberalism_subtype
					traits = { eco_bank_president }
				}
			}
			if = { # Clarence D. Martin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_martin
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Clarence D. Martin"
					desc = "POLITICS_CLARENCE_MARTIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Clarence_Martin.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = soclib_humanistic_capitalism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_taming_the_west }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles A. Sprague
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_sprague
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles A. Sprague"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_SPRAGUE_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Charles_A_Sprague.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = soclib_humanistic_capitalism_subtype
					traits = { economic_reformer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Manchester Boddy
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_boddy
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Manchester Boddy"
					desc = "POLITICS_MANCHESTOR_BODDY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Manchester_Boddy.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = centrist_subtype
					traits = { editor }
				}
			}
			if = { # John F Aiso
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_aiso
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Fujio Aiso"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_AISO_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_John_Aiso_Civ.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = centrist_subtype
					traits = { judge_aiso }
				}
			}
			if = { # Robert Taft
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_taft
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Robert Taft"
					desc = "POLITICS_Robert_Taft_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Robert_A_Taft.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = libertarian_subtype
					traits = { staunch_constitutionalist }
				}
			}
			
			if = { # Harry Chandler
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_chandler
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry Chandler"
					desc = "POLITICS_HARRY_CHANDLER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Harry_Chandler.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = marlib_christian_democracy_subtype
					traits = { eco_industrialiser }
				}
			}

			if = { # Howard Hughes
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_hughes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Howard Hughes"
					desc = "POLITICS_HOWARD_HUGES_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Howard_Hughes_Hat.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = marlib_oligarchy_subtype
					traits = { captain_of_industry }
				}
				if = {	
					limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Howard Hughes" ruling_only = yes } }
					set_country_leader_portrait = {
						portrait = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Howard_Hughes_Hat.png"
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = { # Frank Merriam
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_merriam
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frank Merriam"
					desc = "POLITICS_FRANK_MERRIAM_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Frank_Merrimam.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = liberal_conservative_subtype
					traits = { PSA_champion_of_the_establishment }
				}
			}
			if = { # Frank Knox
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_knox
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frank Knox"
					desc = "POLITICS_FRANK_KNOX_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Frank_Knox.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = marlib_national_liberalism_subtype
					traits = { eco_balanced_budget_economy }
				}
			}
			if = { # Louis B Meyer
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_meyer
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Louis B. Mayer"
					desc = "POLITICS_LOUIS_B_MEYER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Louis_B_Mayer.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = marlib_hamiltonianism_subtype
					traits = { sec_media_magnate }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles Curtis

country_event = { # Democratic-Republicans Join the Progressives
	id = pacificstates.6000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.6000"}
	title = pacificstates.6000.t
	desc = pacificstates.6000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	tag = CAL
	NOT = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_dem_rep_system
		}
	}

	option = { # Good
		name = pacificstates.6000.a
		add_political_power = 45
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = -0.06 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = CAL_dem_rep_system
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			long_name = CAL_prog_dominance_long
			name = CAL_prog_dominance_party }	
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6006
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

			name = CAL_liberal_dominance_party }
		set_country_flag = PSA_Conservatives_Win
		}
	}

### 1940 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1940 Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.7"}
	title = pacificstates.7.t
	desc = { # Progressive won in 1940
		text = pacificstates.7.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive won in 1940
		text = pacificstates.7.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		tag = CAL
		date > 1940.1.1
		has_country_flag = PSA_1937_election_occured
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_pacific_prosperity
			has_completed_focus = CAL_nation_of_visionaries
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.8
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes

    option = { # Keep the President
		name = pacificstates.7.a
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	option = { # Homer Bone
		name = pacificstates.7.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_bone
		}
	}
	option = { # Sheridan Downey
		name = pacificstates.7.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_downey
		}
	}
	option = { # Henry Wallace
		name = pacificstates.7.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
		}
	}
	option = { # Oswald West
		name = pacificstates.7.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_west
		}
	}
	option = { # Huey Long
		name = pacificstates.7.g
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_support_long
			PAR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Señor Largo"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_long
		}
	}
}

		name = pacificstates.11.a
		set_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
			if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
			set_country_flag = CAL_social_democrats_win_twice_flag
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Ralph_Johnson_Bunche_for_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
				if = {
					limit = {
					NOT = {

						}
					}

					limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
					set_country_leader_ideology = georgism_subtype
				    }
					hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
					id = KX_california.50
					days = 42
					}
					}
				}
			}

				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_Homer_Bone_hog_sde

				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
					set_country_leader_ideology = socdem_agrarianism_subtype
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_downey

				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_Sheridan_Downey_hog_sde

### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1944 Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.12"}
	title = pacificstates.12.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = pacificstates.12.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.12.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}	
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_pacific_prosperity
			has_completed_focus = CAL_nation_of_visionaries
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = pacificstates.12.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_progressive_primary_taylor
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.12.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 Commonwealth Primary
	id = pacificstates.15001
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.15001"}
	title = pacificstates.15001.t
	desc = { # Commonwealth Party won the presidency just last time
		text = pacificstates.15001.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
	desc = { # Commonwealth Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.15001.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	immediate = {
	set_country_flag = Dem_survive
	}
	
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}	
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_pacific_prosperity
			has_completed_focus = CAL_nation_of_visionaries
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.15001.a
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.02 }
	}
	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = pacificstates.15001.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
		}
	}
	option = { # Culbert Olson
		name = pacificstates.15001.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_commonwealth_primary_olson
		}
	}
	option = { # Charlie Chaplin
		name = pacificstates.15001.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAL_immigrant_presidents
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_commonwealth_primary_chaplin
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Robert Heinlein
		name = pacificstates.15001.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_commonwealth_primary_heinlein
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democrat Party won also in 1940
		text = pacificstates.15.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Democrat Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.15.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}	
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_pacific_prosperity
			has_completed_focus = CAL_nation_of_visionaries
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Daniel I. J. Thornton
		name = pacificstates.15.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_democrat_primary_thornton
		}
	}
	option = { # Bourke B. Hickenlooper
		name = pacificstates.15.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_democratic_primary_hickenlooper
		}
	}
	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = pacificstates.15.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}
}

				id = pacificstates.17
				days = 1276
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.18
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.19
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.20
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}
}

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###

country_event = { # 1948 Commonwealth Primary
	id = pacificstates.17005
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.17005"}
	title = pacificstates.17005.t
	desc = { # Commonwealth Party won the presidency just last time
		text = pacificstates.17005.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
	}
	desc = { # Commonwealth Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.17005.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	immediate = {
	set_country_flag = Dem_survive
	}
	
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}	
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = CAL_pacific_prosperity
			has_completed_focus = CAL_nation_of_visionaries
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.17005.a
		trigger = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.02 }
	}
	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = pacificstates.17005.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
		}
	}
	option = { # Culbert Olson
		name = pacificstates.17005.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_commonwealth_primary_olson
		}
	}
	option = { # Charlie Chaplin
		name = pacificstates.17005.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CAL_immigrant_presidents
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_commonwealth_primary_chaplin
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Robert Heinlein
		name = pacificstates.17005.e
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_commonwealth_primary_heinlein
		}
	}
}

			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_election_republican
			if = {
			limit = { has_government = market_liberal NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_republicans_win_twice } }
			set_country_flag = CAL_republicans_win_twice
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Richard Nixon
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_republican_primary_nixon
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_Richard_Nixon_hog_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Barry_Morris_Goldwater_eco_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Ray_Lyman_Wilbur_sec_mli
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
					set_country_leader_ideology = marlib_national_liberalism_subtype
				}
			}
			if = { # James Dean
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_republican_primary_dean
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_James_Dean_hog_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Barry_Morris_Goldwater_eco_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Ray_Lyman_Wilbur_sec_mli
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
					set_country_leader_ideology = marlib_radical_liberalism_subtype
				}
			}
			if = { # George N. Craig
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_republican_primary_craig
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_George_N_Craig_hog_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_John_Foster_Dulles_for_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Barry_Morris_Goldwater_eco_mli
				add_ideas = CAL_Ray_Lyman_Wilbur_sec_mli
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
					set_country_leader_ideology = progressive_democracy_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Democrat
		name = pacificstates.21.e
		set_country_flag = PSA_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_election_democrat
			if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_conservative NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_democrats_won_twice_flag } }
			set_country_flag = CAL_democrats_won_twice_flag
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Val Peterson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1948_democratic_primary_peterson
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = CAL_Val_Peterson_hog_sco
				add_ideas = CAL_Henry_Morgenthau_Jr_for_sco
				add_ideas = CAL_William_Myron_Keck_eco_sco
				add_ideas = CAL_Claude_A_Watson_sec_sco
			}
			if = { # Harry P. Cain
				limit = {

				}

				add_ideas = CAL_Harry_P_Cain_hog_sco

					set_country_leader_ideology = conservative_populism_subtype

		}

	option = { # Radicals

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_election_radicals

### Foreign Policy 22 - 49###
country_event = { # America is reunited
	id = pacificstates.22
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.22"}
	title = pacificstates.22.t
	desc = pacificstates.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		NOT = {
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = COR
			AND = {
				country_exists = NEE
				NEE = { 
					has_country_flag = NEE_claimed_america
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = TXS
				TXS = { 
					has_country_flag = TXS_claimed_america
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = NYC
				NYC = {
					has_country_flag = NYC_can_invade_america
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = BBR
				BBR = {	
					has_country_flag = BBR_claimed_america
					is_ally_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
		}
		owns_state = 361 #Maryland
		owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
		owns_state = 395 #Illinois
		owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
		owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
		has_war = no		
	}

	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		name = pacificstates.22.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAl_peaceoutgang
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = PSA_reunited_america_flag
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_JAP_USA
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAL_JAP_USA
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_country_flag = USA_SPIRITUALIST
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = USA_SPIRITUALIST
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAL_Norton_PSA
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		has_cosmetic_tag = CAL_wallace_shambhala
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAL_wallace_shambhala_usa
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag
		}
		has_government = radical_socialist
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CAL_USA_EPIC
		}
		if = {
		limit = {
		NOT = {
		OR = {
		has_government = radical_socialist
		has_country_flag = USA_SPIRITUALIST
		has_country_flag = CAL_JAP_USA
		has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag
		has_country_flag = CAL_Wallace_Shalala
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			remove_ACW_cores = yes
		}
	    }
	}
	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		name = pacificstates.22.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAl_peaceoutgang
		}
		country_event = calpeaceout.11
	}
}

		}

		}

	desc = pacificstates.40.d

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_country_flag = PSA_reunited_america_flag
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		count_triggers = {
			amount = 2
			owns_state = 361
			owns_state = 797
			owns_state = 378
			owns_state = 373
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = { # Washington DC
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 361
		}
		name = pacificstates.40.a
		set_capital = { state = 361 }
	}
	option = { # San Francisco
		name = pacificstates.40.b
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 797
		}
		set_capital = { state = 797 }
	}
	option = { # Sacremento
		name = pacificstates.40.c
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 378
		}
		set_capital = { state = 378 }
	}
	option = { # Saint Louis

			owns_state = 373
		}
		set_capital = { state = 373 }
	}
	option = { # Stay put
		name = pacificstates.40.f
	}
}

### Domestic Policy Events 50 - 75 ###
country_event = { # Formation of HUAC
	id = pacificstates.50
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.50"}
	title = pacificstates.50.t
	desc = pacificstates.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
		tag = CAL
		tag = USA
		}
		OR = {
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_completed_focus = CAL_red_scare
		}
	}

	option = { # HUAC is Formed
		name = pacificstates.50.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
	option = { # HUAC is not Formed
		name = pacificstates.50.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { # Anti-Klan Laws
	id = pacificstates.56
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.56"}
	title = pacificstates.56.t
	desc = pacificstates.56.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CAL
			tag = USA
		}
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 200
	}

	option = { # Flavor
		name = pacificstates.56.a
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = -0.02 }
	}
	option = { # Flavor
		name = pacificstates.56.b
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

	desc = pacificstates.62.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_government = social_conservative
		has_completed_focus = CAL_immigration_act
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = pacificstates.62.a
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAL
				is_controlled_by = CAL
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
	option = {
		name = pacificstates.62.b
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.01 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Trial of the Weapons companies
	id = pacificstates.66
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.66"}
	title = pacificstates.66.t
	desc = pacificstates.66.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_reconstruction

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.67
				days = 7
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.68
				days = 14
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.69
				days = 21
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.70
				days = 28
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # companies allowed
		name = pacificstates.66.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
	}
	option = { # companies not allowed
		name = pacificstates.66.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

country_event = { # Zoot Suit Riots(PSA)
	id = pacificstates.103
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.103"}
	title = pacificstates.103.t
	desc = pacificstates.103.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		has_war = yes
		any_enemy_country = {
			is_actual_major = yes
		}
		798 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}

	option = { # Flavor
		name = pacificstates.103.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = MEX
				}
				MEX = {
					country_event = {
						id = pacificstates.104
						days = 3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = {
		has_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_both
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_both
			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {# I like it how it is
		name = pacificstates.203.b

			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

	option = {# Cool Hap
	name = pacificstates.229.a
				set_country_flag = CAL_million_sons
				set_country_flag = LEADER_GUI_VISIBLE

				set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						name = CAL_arnold_party
						long_name = CAL_arnold_party_long
				}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "George Marshall"
			desc = "CAL_DADDY_MARSHALL_ARMY_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_george_marshall.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = authdem_junta_subtype
			traits = { quartermaster_general }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			CAL_Henry_Arnold_hog_ade
			CAL_James_Doolittle_for_ade
			CAL_George_Marshall_eco_ade
			CAL_Chester_Nimitz_sec_ade
		}
		if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = CAL_Spiritualist_Aid }
			country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.351
			days = 1
				}
			}
		else = {
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.246
			days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		
	}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.246"}
	title = pacificstates.246.t
	desc = pacificstates.246.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_police2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {# Their tyranny finally ends
		name = pacificstates.246.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = -0.03 }
		add_manpower = -2000
		WCC = {
		add_manpower = 2000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.247
			days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {# MacArthur's Demands
	id = pacificstates.247
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.247"}
	title = pacificstates.247.t
	desc = pacificstates.247.d
	picture = GFX_mac_4

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {# 
		name = pacificstates.247.a
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.247
			days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {# I like it how it is
		name = pacificstates.247.b
		declare_war_on = {
			target = USA
			type = annex_everything
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = WCC
			type = annex_everything
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = CSA
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = TXS_ACW_CAL
			}
			TXS = {
				declare_war_on = {
				target = USA
				type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
				target = CSA
				type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
				target = WCC
				type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.247
			days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

				}
			}
			CAL = { declare_war_on = { target = TEX type = annex_everything	} }
		}
		every_state = {

			}

		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KX_california.16" }
	title = KX_california.18.t
	desc = KX_california.18.d
	picture = Jap_coup

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = KX_california.18.a
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				add_to_faction = CAL
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Tamon Yamaguchi"
				desc = "POLITICS_TAMON_YAMAGUCHI_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Tamon_Yamaguchi.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = autocratic_colonial_govt_subtype
				traits = {
					appointed_from_tokyo
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				last_election = "1936.11.16"
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = CAL_japan_junta_party_long
				name = CAL_japan_junta_party
			}
			set_country_flag = CAL_JAP_USA
			clr_country_flag = USA_SPIRITUALIST
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = JAP_Ministers_Allowed
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CAL_Tamon_Yamaguchi_hog_npo
					CAL_Isoroku_Yamamoto_for_npo
					CAL_Chuichi_Nagumo_eco_npo
					CAL_Shiro_Ishii_sec_npo
				}
				create_country_leader = {# Earl Warren
					name = "Earl Warren"
					desc = "POLITICS_EARL_WARREN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Earl_Warren.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = radical_liberalism_subtype
					traits = { PSA_crusader_of_justice }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

		}

			name = "Shirō Ishii"

				remove_idea = CAL_JAP_Integration_2
				add_idea = CAL_JAP_Integration_4
			}
		}
		else = {
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAL_JAP_Integration_3
			add_idea = CAL_JAP_Integration_4
		}
	    }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KX_california.26
				days = 908
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = KX_california.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KX_california.25" }
	title = KX_california.27.t
	desc = KX_california.27.d
	picture = GFX_CAL_Vegas_Event_1

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_rebuilding_vegas
		NOT = {
			has_idea = CAL_Vegas_rebuliding
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = KX_california.27.a
		add_political_power = 100
		379 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = air_base
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = anti_air_building
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_resource = { type = tungsten amount = 3 state = 379 }
		add_resource = { type = steel amount = 3 state = 379 }
		add_resource = { type = chromium amount = 3 state = 379 }
		add_resource = { type = oil amount = 3 state = 379 }
	}
}

		has_global_flag = CAl_peaceoutgang
		has_global_flag = CAL_fuckit_free_cali
		has_global_flag = TXS_ACW_CAL
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {# 
		name = calpeaceout.21.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = COR
			}
			COR = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			CSA = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			USA = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = WCC
			}
			WCC = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = TEX
			}
			TEX = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAL_TXS_loyalty_tooltip
	}
	option = {# 
		name = calpeaceout.21.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = COR
			}
			COR = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CSA
			}
			CSA = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = USA
			}
			USA = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = WCC
			}
			WCC = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = TEX
			}
			TEX = {
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = TXS_ACW_CAL
		clr_global_flag = TXS_FACTION
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAL_TXS_choose_faction_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #begone California
	id = calpeaceout.22
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event calpeaceout.2" }
	title = calpeaceout.22.t
	desc = calpeaceout.22.d
	picture = GFX_CAL_legislature 

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = calpeaceout.22.a #fine
		add_political_power = 150
		add_stability = -0.1
		378 = {
			set_state_name = "Jefferson"
		}
		829 = {
			set_state_name = "Mojave"
		}

	}
	option = {
		name = calpeaceout.22.b #fuck no
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
		add_stability = -0.25
		378 = {
			set_state_name = "Jefferson"
		}
		829 = {
			set_state_name = "Mojave"
		}
		798 = {
			set_state_name = "Angels"
		}
		797 = {
			set_state_name = "Frisco"
			set_state_flag = CAL_renamed_state_frisco
		}
	}	

	option = {
		name = calpeaceout.22.c #fuck no
		add_stability = 0.05
	}	
}

country_event = { #Japan peaceout
	id = calpeaceout.23
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event calpeaceout.3" }
	title = calpeaceout.23.t
	desc = calpeaceout.23.d
	picture = GFX_CAL_legislature 

	trigger= {
		has_war_with = CAL
		CAL = { 
			is_ai = yes 
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			has_capitulated = yes
		}
		JAP = { is_ai = yes }
		controls_state = 378
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = calpeaceout.23.a #yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAL
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = CAL
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_on_continent = north_america
				is_owned_by = JAP
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = calpeaceout.23.b #no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}	
}
